It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_CHANNEL = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per token. It's computed on-the-fly.\n    PER_TOKEN = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per group. It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_GROUP = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in INT8.\n    INT8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in FP8.\n    FP8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # FP8 QDQ\n    FP8_QDQ = auto()\n    # FP8 rowwise\n    FP8_ROWWISE = auto()\n    # FP8 block scales for Deepseek\n    FP8_1x128_128x128 = auto()\n    # W4A8 qserve\n    W4A8_QSERVE = auto()\n    # FP4\n    NVFP4 = auto()\n    NVFP4_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # W4A8 NVFP4\n    W4A8_NVFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    # W4A8 MXFP4\n    W4A8_MXFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    W4A8_MXFP4_INT8 = auto()\n    W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8 = auto()\n    W4A16_MXFP4 = auto()\n\n    # The smallest power-of-two that is not used by a flag. f\"{quantize_activations=}, \"\n                             f\"{per_token=}, \"\n                             f\"{per_channel=}, \"\n                             f\"{per_group=}, \"\n QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n\n        # Do we quantize the activations?\n        if quantize_activations:\n            mode = mode | QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS\n\n        # Per-channel/per-token/per-group It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_CHANNEL = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per token. It's computed on-the-fly.\n    PER_TOKEN = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per group.
